<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> delicious, appetizing</li>

<p>Per Vasmer, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мека́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mekátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to understand, to think <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mekati</i>, derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> by analogy with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смекать.html>смека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смекнуть.html>смекну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually  intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to understand, to get it, to catch on, to realize
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекать.html>смека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>чём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smekátʹ</b> v čóm délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get it, to get the point</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смелость.html>сме́лость</a> (5719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смелый.html>сме́лый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smélyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bold, courageous</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смелость.html>сме́лость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smélostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смелость.html>сме́лости</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>boldness, courage; audacity</li></ol>

<p><b>сме́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лость</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-сме-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-л-ость</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***смелый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смелый.html>смелый</a> (2470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съмѣлъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭmělŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъmělъ</i>; synchronically, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметь.html>сметь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smetʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dare</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:смелый.html>смел</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smel</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">smělý</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">śmiały</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смелый.html>сме́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smélyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)смеле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)смеле́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>courageous, daring, audacious, bold, brave</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***смена.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смена.html>сме́на</a> (2059)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смена.html>сме́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sména</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смена.html>сме́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смена.html>сме́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смена.html>сме́н</a></b>)

<ol><li>change, replacement</li>
<li>shift</li>

***сменить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сменить.html>смени́ть</a> (2921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мени́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-menítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменить.html>смени́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smenítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменять.html>сменя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change, to replace
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сменить.html>смени́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ру</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smenítʹ</b> kvartíru</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move house</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to succeed (to come after)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смениться.html>смени́ться</a> (6331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменить.html>смени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смениться.html>смени́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smenítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменяться.html>сменя́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меняться.html>меня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to change into (+ instrumental)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испуг.html>испу́г</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смениться.html>смени́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достью</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ispúg <b>smenílsja</b> rádostʹju.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Fear turned to joy.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to alternate, to take turns</li>
<li>to be relieved (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from a work shift)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смениться.html>смени́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дежурство.html>дежу́рства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smenítʹsja</b> s dežúrstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go off duty</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменить.html>смени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***сменный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сменный.html>сме́нный</a> (23056)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смена.html>сме́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sména</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменный.html>сме́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sménnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shift <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">work, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>replaceable, removable</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменить.html>смени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменять.html>сменя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменить.html>смени́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to change, to replace
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сменять.html>сменя́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:квартира.html>кварти́ру</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smenjátʹ</b> kvartíru</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to move house</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to succeed (to come after)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сменять.html>сменя́ющий</a> (11378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменять.html>сменя́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smenjájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сменять.html>сменя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smenjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>сме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня́<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ю<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>щий</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>Прича́стие</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мен-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-я-ющ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b>.
